 bhartiya captain mahendra singh dhoni ne england ke khilaaf lagaataar do match main badi jeet kaa shrey kaaphi had tak yuva khilaadiyon ko dete hue somvaar ko ki kai bade naamon kii anupasthiti main in cricketron ne apni bhoomika acchhee tarah se nibhaai he
 Dhoni said after a convincing eight-wicket win in the second match, victory is always important and when this victory is won on the strength of the youth, it becomes special
 mujhe khushi he ki yuva khilaadiyon ne jarurat ke samay acha pradarshan kiya
 We are expecting him to perform like he did with bat and ball at the international level
 bhartiya captain ne visheshkar rup se tej gendbaaj aar vinayakumar, umesh yadav, viraat kohli or spinneron kaa zikr kiya
 He said, the credit of the victory goes to the entire team but the contribution of the youth was important
 bharat is match main sachin tendulkar, virendra sahvaag, yuvaraj singh, jahir khan jaise khilaadiyon kii anupasthiti main khel rahaa he
 Dhoni said of Kohli, he really batted very well
 vah yuva he or use upree kram main ballebaaji karne ke adhik maukey die janaa jaruri tha taaki use acchhee shuruyaat ko bade score main tabdeel karne kaa mauka mil jaae
 He still needs improvement but i am confident that the way he has continued to improve his game over time, he will do so even further
 dhoni ne kaha, gambhir kii number teen par pari kaaphi mahatvapurn rahi
 England bowlers were getting light swing at that time and in such a situation it was important to stay on the wicket
 gautam ne shandaar pari kheli
 The partnership between him and Kohli actually made the match somewhat unilateral
 unhone yadav ke bare main kaha ki vah lagaataar 130 or 140 kimi kii gati se gendbaaji kar rahaa he
 But speed is not everything
 use sateekta, jarurat padane par bounsar, yarker or bairieshan bhi seekhney honge
 Hopefully, he will continue to learn these when he gets experience
 iske saath hi use chot se bhi bachanaa hoga taaki vah chot ke kaaran kabhi koi match miss nahin kare
 Dhoni said, we cannot forget Vinaykumar and Praveen's contribution
 unhone hamen shuru main hi safalataa dilaayi or phir gendbaajon ne kisi bhi samay lambii saajhedaari nahin banane di
 It was very important
 dhoni se jab poocha gaya ki bharat apni sarajameen par acchhee jeet darj kar rahaa he jabaki england main aisa nahin kar paaya, unhone kaha, main iskaa ek kaaran nahin bataa saktaa
 There can be many reasons for this

 in jeet main coach dancan flachar ke yogadan ke bare main unhone kaha, flachar ne kaaphi prabhaav daalaa he
